    19	package event
    20	
    21	import (
    22	        "context"
    23	        goerrors "errors"
    24	        "strings"
    25	
    26	        "github.com/pkg/errors"
    27	        "github.com/submariner-io/admiral/pkg/log"
    28	        "k8s.io/utils/set"
    29	        logf "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/log"
    30	)
    31	
    32	type Registry struct {
    33	        name          string
    34	        networkPlugin string
    35	        eventHandlers []Handler
    36	}
    37	
    38	var logger = log.Logger{Logger: logf.Log.WithName("EventRegistry")}
    39	
    40	// NewRegistry creates a new registry with the given name, typically referencing the owner, to manage event
    41	// Handlers that match the given networkPlugin name. The given event Handlers whose associated network plugin matches the given
    42	// networkPlugin name are added. Non-matching Handlers are ignored. Handlers will be called in registration order.
    43	func NewRegistry(ctx context.Context, name, networkPlugin string, eventHandlers ...Handler) (*Registry, error) {
    44	        r := &Registry{
    45	                name:          name,
    46	                networkPlugin: strings.ToLower(networkPlugin),
    47	                eventHandlers: []Handler{},
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        for _, eventHandler := range eventHandlers {
    51	                err := r.addHandler(ctx, eventHandler)
    52	                if err != nil {
    53	                        return nil, err
    54	                }
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        return r, nil
    58	}
    59	
    60	// GetName returns the name of the registry.
    61	func (er *Registry) GetName() string {
    62	        return er.name
    63	}
    64	
    65	func (er *Registry) addHandler(ctx context.Context, eventHandler Handler) error {
    66	        evNetworkPlugins := set.New[string]()
    67	
    68	        for _, np := range eventHandler.GetNetworkPlugins() {
    69	                evNetworkPlugins.Insert(strings.ToLower(np))
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        if er.networkPlugin == AnyNetworkPlugin || evNetworkPlugins.Has(AnyNetworkPlugin) || evNetworkPlugins.Has(er.networkPlugin) {
    73	                if err := eventHandler.Init(ctx); err != nil {
    74	                        return errors.Wrapf(err, "Event handler %q failed to initialize", eventHandler.GetName())
    75	                }
    76	
    77	                er.eventHandlers = append(er.eventHandlers, eventHandler)
    78	                logger.Infof("Event handler %q added to registry %q.", eventHandler.GetName(), er.name)
    79	        } else {
    80	                logger.V(log.DEBUG).Infof("Event handler %q ignored for registry %q as networkPlugin is %q.",
    81	                        eventHandler.GetName(), er.name, er.networkPlugin)
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        return nil
    85	}
    86	
    87	func (er *Registry) GetHandlers() []Handler {
    88	        return er.eventHandlers
    89	}
    90	
    91	func (er *Registry) StopHandlers() error {
    92	        return er.invokeHandlers("Stop", func(h Handler) error {
    93	                return h.Stop()
    94	        })
    95	}
    96	
    97	func (er *Registry) Uninstall() error {
    98	        return er.invokeHandlers("Uninstall", func(h Handler) error {
    99	                return h.Uninstall()
   100	        })
   101	}
   102	
   103	func (er *Registry) invokeHandlers(eventName string, invoke func(h Handler) error) error {
   104	        var errs []error
   105	
   106	        for _, h := range er.eventHandlers {
   107	                err := invoke(h)
   108	                if err != nil {
   109	                        errs = append(errs, errors.Wrapf(err, "%q returned error", h.GetName()))
   110	                }
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        return errors.Wrapf(goerrors.Join(errs...), "%s failed", eventName)
   114	}
   115

   146

   231	func getTCPMssValue(localNode *corev1.Node) int {
   232	        tcpMssStr := localNode.GetAnnotations()[v1.TCPMssValue]
   233	
   234	        if tcpMssStr == "" {
   235	                return 0
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        tcpMssValue, err := strconv.Atoi(tcpMssStr)
   239	        if err != nil {
   240	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error parsing %q annotation", v1.TCPMssValue)
   241	                return 0
   242	        }
   243	
   244	        return tcpMssValue
   245	}

    46	type Config struct {
    47	        pinger.ControllerConfig
    48	        HealthCheckerEnabled     bool
    49	        RouteAgentUpdateInterval time.Duration
    50	        RouteAgentOwner          metav1.Object
    51	        Namespace                string
    52	        LocalNodeName            string
    53	        Version                  string
    54	}
    55	
    56	type controller struct {
    57	        event.HandlerBase
    58	        pingerController pinger.Controller
    59	        config           Config
    60	        stopCh           chan struct{}
    61	        stopOnce         sync.Once
    62	        client           v1typed.RouteAgentInterface
    63	}
    64	
    65	var logger = log.Logger{Logger: logf.Log.WithName("HealthChecker")}
    66	
    67	func New(config *Config, client v1typed.SubmarinerV1Interface) event.Handler {
    68	        return &controller{
    69	                pingerController: pinger.NewController(config.ControllerConfig),
    70	                config:           *config,
    71	                client:           client.RouteAgents(config.Namespace),
    72	                stopCh:           make(chan struct{}),
    73	        }
    74	}
    75	
    76	func (h *controller) Stop() error {
    77	        h.pingerController.Stop()
    78	
    79	        h.stopOnce.Do(func() {
    80	                close(h.stopCh)
    81	        })
    82	
    83	        err := h.client.Delete(context.TODO(),
    84	                h.config.LocalNodeName, metav1.DeleteOptions{})
    85	        if err != nil && !apiError.IsNotFound(err) {
    86	                return errors.Wrapf(err, "Error deleting RouteAgent: %s", h.config.LocalNodeName)
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        return nil
    90	}
    91	
    92	func (h *controller) RemoteEndpointCreated(endpoint *submarinerv1.Endpoint) error {
    93	        return h.onRemoteEndpint(endpoint, "created")
    94	}
    95	
    96	func (h *controller) RemoteEndpointUpdated(endpoint *submarinerv1.Endpoint) error {
    97	        return h.onRemoteEndpint(endpoint, "updated")
    98	}

    19	package ovn
    20	
    21	import (
    22	        "context"
    23	
    24	        "github.com/pkg/errors"
    25	        "github.com/submariner-io/admiral/pkg/util"
    26	        nodeutil "github.com/submariner-io/submariner/pkg/node"
    27	        "github.com/submariner-io/submariner/pkg/packetfilter"
    28	        "github.com/submariner-io/submariner/pkg/routeagent_driver/chains"
    29	        "github.com/submariner-io/submariner/pkg/routeagent_driver/constants"
    30	        "github.com/submariner-io/submariner/pkg/routeagent_driver/handlers/ovn/vsctl"
    31	        corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
    32	        metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
    33	        k8snet "k8s.io/utils/net"
    34	)
    35	
    36	func (ovn *Handler) Stop() error {
    37	        ovn.gatewayRouteController.stop()
    38	
    39	        if ovn.nonGatewayRouteController != nil {
    40	                ovn.nonGatewayRouteController.stop()
    41	        }
    42	
    43	        close(ovn.stopCh)
    44	
    45	        return nil
    46	}
    47	
    48	func (ovn *Handler) Uninstall() error {
    49	        logger.Infof("Uninstalling OVN components from the node")
    50	
    51	        err := ovn.cleanupRoutes()
    52	        if err != nil {
    53	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error cleaning the routes")
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        err = ovn.netLink.FlushRouteTable(constants.RouteAgentInterClusterNetworkTableID)
    57	        if err != nil {
    58	                logger.Errorf(err, "Flushing routing table %d returned error",
    59	                        constants.RouteAgentInterClusterNetworkTableID)
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        err = ovn.netLink.FlushRouteTable(constants.RouteAgentHostNetworkTableID)
    63	        if err != nil {
    64	                logger.Errorf(err, "Flushing routing table %d returned error",
    65	                        constants.RouteAgentHostNetworkTableID)
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        ovn.deleteIPHookChain(packetfilter.TableTypeFilter, chains.NewForwarding())
    69	        ovn.deleteIPHookChain(packetfilter.TableTypeFilter, chains.NewForwardingMSSClamp())
    70	        ovn.deleteIPHookChain(packetfilter.TableTypeNAT, chains.NewPostRouting())
    71	
    72	        err = util.Update[*corev1.Node](context.TODO(), ovn.nodeResourceInterface(), &corev1.Node{
    73	                ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{Name: nodeutil.GetLocalNodeName()},
    74	        }, func(existing *corev1.Node) (*corev1.Node, error) {
    75	                delete(existing.Annotations, OVNKSNATExcludeSubnetsAnnotation)
    76	                return existing, nil
    77	        })
    78	        if err != nil {
    79	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error removing node annotation %q", OVNKSNATExcludeSubnetsAnnotation)
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        return nil
    83	}
    84	
    85	func (ovn *Handler) deleteIPHookChain(table packetfilter.TableType, chain *packetfilter.ChainIPHook) {
    86	        if err := ovn.pFilter.ClearChain(table, chain.Name); err != nil {
    87	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error clearing IP hook chain %q from %q table", chain.Name, table)
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        if err := ovn.pFilter.DeleteIPHookChain(chain); err != nil {
    91	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error deleting IP hook chain %q from %q table", chain.Name, table)
    92	        }
    93	}
    94	
    95	func (ovn *Handler) cleanupRoutes() error {
    96	        rules, err := ovn.netLink.RuleList(k8snet.IPv4)
    97	        if err != nil {
    98	                return errors.Wrapf(err, "error listing rules")
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        for i := range rules {
   102	                if rules[i].Table == constants.RouteAgentInterClusterNetworkTableID || rules[i].Table == constants.RouteAgentHostNetworkTableID {
   103	                        err = ovn.netLink.RuleDel(&rules[i])
   104	                        if err != nil {
   105	                                return errors.Wrapf(err, "error deleting the rule %v", rules[i])
   106	                        }
   107	                }
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        return nil
   111	}
   112	
   113	func (ovn *Handler) LegacyCleanup() {
   114	        err := vsctl.DelInternalPort(ovnK8sSubmarinerBridge, ovnK8sSubmarinerInterface)
   115	        if err != nil {
   116	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error deleting Submariner port %q", ovnK8sSubmarinerInterface)
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        err = vsctl.DelBridge(ovnK8sSubmarinerBridge)
   120	        if err != nil {
   121	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error deleting Submariner bridge %q", ovnK8sSubmarinerBridge)
   122	        }
   123	}

   223	func (h *mtuHandler) RemoteEndpointRemoved(endpoint *submV1.Endpoint) error {
   224	        logger.Infof("Processing removed Endpoint %q", endpoint.Spec.CableName)
   225	
   226	        subnets := cidr.ExtractSubnets(h.ipFamily, endpoint.Spec.Subnets)
   227	        for _, subnet := range subnets {
   228	                logError(h.remoteIPSet.DelEntry(subnet), "Error deleting the subnet %q from the remote IPSet", subnet)
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        return nil
   232	}

   241	        logger.Infof("Flushing packetfilter entries in %q chain of table type %q", chains.SmPostRoutingMss, h.tableType.String())
   242	
   243	        logError(h.pFilter.ClearChain(h.tableType, chains.SmPostRoutingMss),
   244	                "Error flushing chain %q of table type %q", chains.SmPostRoutingMss, h.tableType.String())
   245

   247	
   248	        logError(h.pFilter.DeleteIPHookChain(&packetfilter.ChainIPHook{
   249	                Name:     chains.SmPostRoutingMss,
   250	                Type:     h.chainType,
   251	                Hook:     packetfilter.ChainHookPostrouting,
   252	                Priority: packetfilter.ChainPriorityFirst,
   253	        }), "Error deleting IP hook chain %q of table type %q", chains.SmPostRoutingMss, h.tableType.String())
   254	
   255	        logError(h.localIPSet.Flush(), "Error flushing ipset %q", h.localCIDRIPSet)
   256	
   257	        logError(h.localIPSet.Destroy(), "Error deleting ipset %q", h.localCIDRIPSet)
   258	
   259	        logError(h.remoteIPSet.Flush(), "Error flushing ipset %q", h.remoteCIDRIPSet)
   260	
   261	        logError(h.remoteIPSet.Destroy(), "Error deleting ipset %q", h.remoteCIDRIPSet)

   130	func (h *calicoIPPoolHandler) TransitionToGateway() error {
   131	        var retErrors []error
   132	        logger.Info("TransitionToGateway")
   133	
   134	        endpoints := h.State().GetRemoteEndpoints()
   135	        for i := range endpoints {
   136	                err := h.createIPPool(&endpoints[i])
   137	                if err != nil {
   138	                        logger.Warningf("Failed to create ippool %s", endpoints[i].GetName())
   139	                        retErrors = append(retErrors,
   140	                                errors.Wrapf(err, "error creating Calico IPPool for endpoint %q ", endpoints[i].GetName()))
   141	                }
   142	        }
   143	
   144	        return goerrors.Join(retErrors...)
   145	}
   146	
   147	func (h *calicoIPPoolHandler) Uninstall() error {
   148	        logger.Info("Uninstalling Calico IPPools used for Submariner")
   149	
   150	        labelSelector := labels.SelectorFromSet(map[string]string{SubmarinerIPPool: "true"}).String()
   151	        err := h.client.ProjectcalicoV3().IPPools().DeleteCollection(context.TODO(), metav1.DeleteOptions{},
   152	                metav1.ListOptions{LabelSelector: labelSelector})
   153	
   154	        if err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
   155	                return errors.Wrapf(err, "Failed to delete Calico IPPools using labelSelector %q", labelSelector)
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        logger.Infof("Successfully delete Calico IPPools using labelSelector %q", labelSelector)
   159	
   160	        if err := h.restoreROKSCalicoCfg(); err != nil {
   161	                return err
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        return nil
   165	}

    33	func (kp *SyncHandler) Uninstall() error {
    34	        logger.Infof("Uninstalling Submariner changes from the node %q", kp.hostname)
    35	        logger.Infof("Flushing route table %d entries", constants.RouteAgentHostNetworkTableID)
    36	
    37	        err := kp.netLink.FlushRouteTable(constants.RouteAgentHostNetworkTableID)
    38	        if err != nil {
    39	                // We can safely ignore this error, as this table will exist only on GW nodes
    40	                logger.V(log.TRACE).Infof("Flushing routing table %d returned error. Can be ignored on non-Gw node: %v",
    41	                        constants.RouteAgentHostNetworkTableID, err)
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        err = kp.netLink.RuleDelIfPresent(netlinkAPI.NewTableRule(constants.RouteAgentHostNetworkTableID, kp.ipFamily))
    45	        if err != nil {
    46	                logger.V(log.TRACE).Infof("Deleting IP Rule pointing to %d table returned error: %v",
    47	                        constants.RouteAgentHostNetworkTableID, err)
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        kp.deleteVxLANInterface()
    51	        kp.deleteIPTableChains()
    52	
    53	        return nil
    54	}
    55	
    56	func (kp *SyncHandler) deleteVxLANInterface() {
    57	        iface := &netlink.Vxlan{
    58	                LinkAttrs: netlink.LinkAttrs{
    59	                        Name:  kp.vxlanIface,
    60	                        Flags: net.FlagUp,
    61	                },
    62	                VxlanId: 100,
    63	                SrcAddr: nil,
    64	                Port:    port.IntraClusterVxLAN,
    65	        }
    66	
    67	        logger.Infof("Deleting the %q interface", kp.vxlanIface)
    68	
    69	        err := netlinkAPI.New().LinkDel(iface)
    70	        if err != nil {
    71	                logger.Errorf(err, "Failed to delete the vxlan interface %q", kp.vxlanIface)
    72	        }
    73	}
    74	
    75	func (kp *SyncHandler) deleteIPTableChains() {
    76	        pFilter, err := packetfilter.New(kp.ipFamily)
    77	        if err != nil {
    78	                logger.Errorf(err, "Failed to initialize packetfilter interface")
    79	                return
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        logger.Infof("Flushing IPv%v packetfilter entries in %q chain of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmPostRouting, constants.NATTable)
    83	
    84	        if err := pFilter.ClearChain(packetfilter.TableTypeNAT, chains.SmPostRouting); err != nil {
    85	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error flushing packetfilter chain %q of %q table", chains.SmPostRouting,
    86	                        constants.NATTable)
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        logger.Infof("Deleting IPv%v packetfilter entry in %q chain of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmPostRouting, constants.NATTable)
    90	
    91	        chain := packetfilter.ChainIPHook{
    92	                Name:     chains.SmPostRouting,
    93	                Type:     packetfilter.ChainTypeNAT,
    94	                Hook:     packetfilter.ChainHookPostrouting,
    95	                Priority: packetfilter.ChainPriorityFirst,
    96	        }
    97	        if err := pFilter.DeleteIPHookChain(&chain); err != nil {
    98	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error deleting IPv%v IPHook chain %q of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmPostRouting,
    99	                        constants.NATTable)
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        logger.Infof("Flushing IPv%v packetfilter entries in %q chain of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmInput, constants.FilterTable)
   103	
   104	        if err := pFilter.ClearChain(packetfilter.TableTypeFilter, chains.SmInput); err != nil {
   105	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error flushing IPv%v packetfilter chain %q of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmInput,
   106	                        constants.FilterTable)
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        logger.Infof("Deleting IPv%v packetfilter entry in %q chain of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmInput, constants.FilterTable)
   110	
   111	        chain = packetfilter.ChainIPHook{
   112	                Name:     chains.SmInput,
   113	                Type:     packetfilter.ChainTypeFilter,
   114	                Hook:     packetfilter.ChainHookInput,
   115	                Priority: packetfilter.ChainPriorityLast,
   116	                JumpRule: &packetfilter.Rule{
   117	                        Proto:       packetfilter.RuleProtoUDP,
   118	                        Action:      packetfilter.RuleActionJump,
   119	                        TargetChain: chains.SmInput,
   120	                },
   121	        }
   122	        if err := pFilter.DeleteIPHookChain(&chain); err != nil {
   123	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error deleting IPv%v IPHook chain %q of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmInput,
   124	                        constants.FilterTable)
   125	        }
   126	
   127	        logger.Infof("Flushing IPv%v packetfilter entries in %q chain of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmSelfSnat, constants.NATTable)
   128	
   129	        if err := pFilter.ClearChain(packetfilter.TableTypeNAT, chains.SmSelfSnat); err != nil {
   130	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error flushing IPv%v packetfilter chain %q of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmSelfSnat,
   131	                        constants.NATTable)
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        chain = packetfilter.ChainIPHook{
   135	                Name:     chains.SmSelfSnat,
   136	                Type:     packetfilter.ChainTypeNAT,
   137	                Hook:     packetfilter.ChainHookPostrouting,
   138	                Priority: packetfilter.ChainPriorityMiddle,
   139	        }
   140	
   141	        if err := pFilter.DeleteIPHookChain(&chain); err != nil {
   142	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error deleting IPv%v IPHook chain %q of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmSelfSnat,
   143	                        constants.NATTable)
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        logger.Infof("Flushing IPv%v packetfilter entries in %q chain of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmForward, constants.FilterTable)
   147	
   148	        if err := pFilter.ClearChain(packetfilter.TableTypeFilter, chains.SmForward); err != nil {
   149	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error flushing IPv%v packetfilter chain %q of %q table", kp.ipFamily, chains.SmForward,
   150	                        constants.FilterTable)
   151	        }
   152

   155	                Type:     packetfilter.ChainTypeFilter,
   156	                Hook:     packetfilter.ChainHookForward,

    84	func (t *TestHandlerBase) FailOnEvent(eventName ...string) {
    85	        for _, e := range eventName {
    86	                t.failOnEvent.Store(e, true)
    87	        }
    88	}
    89	
    90	func (t *TestHandlerBase) checkFailOnEvent(eventName string) error {
    91	        fail, ok := t.failOnEvent.LoadAndDelete(eventName)
    92	        if ok && fail.(bool) {
    93	                return fmt.Errorf("mock handler error for %q", eventName)
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        return nil
    97	}
    98	
    99	func (t *TestHandlerBase) addEvent(eventName string, param any) error {
   100	        if err := t.checkFailOnEvent(eventName); err != nil {
   101	                return err
   102	        }
   103	
   104	        ev := TestEvent{
   105	                Name:      eventName,
   106	                Parameter: param,
   107	                Handler:   t.Name,
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        select {
   111	        case t.Events <- ev:
   112	                return nil
   113	        case <-time.After(5 * time.Second):
   114	                return fmt.Errorf("timeout sending event %q to channel", eventName)
   115	        }
   116	}
   117	
   118	func (t *TestHandlerBase) Init(_ context.Context) error {
   119	        t.Initialized = true
   120	        return t.checkFailOnEvent(EvInit)
   121	}

   124	        return t.Name

    55	func NewGatewayMonitor(ctx context.Context, config *GatewayMonitorConfig) (Interface, error) {
    56	        // We'll panic if config is nil, this is intentional
    57	        gatewayMonitor := &gatewayMonitor{
    58	                baseController:       newBaseController(),
    59	                GatewayMonitorConfig: *config,
    60	                shuttingDown:         atomic.Bool{},
    61	                leaderElectionInfo:   atomic.Pointer[LeaderElectionInfo]{},
    62	        }
    63	
    64	        // When transitioning to a non-gateway or shutting down, the GatewayMonitor cancels leader election which causes it to release the lock,
    65	        // which clears the HolderIdentity field and sets LeaseDuration to one second. This enables the next instance to quickly acquire the
    66	        // lock. However, if the controller instance crashes and doesn't properly release the lock, the next instance will have to await the
    67	        // LeaseDuration period before acquiring the lock. So we don't want LeaseDuration set too high, and we don't want it too low either to
    68	        // give the current instance enough time to complete stopping its controllers.
    69	        //
    70	        // The K8s leader election functionality periodically renews the lease. If it can't be renewed prior to the RenewDeadline, it stops.
    71	        // For our usage, we don't have instances concurrently vying for leadership, so we really don't need to keep renewing the lease. Ideally
    72	        // we would set the RenewDeadline very high to essentially disable it, but it needs to be less than the LeaseDuration setting which we
    73	        // don't want too high.
    74	
    75	        gatewayMonitor.LocalCIDRs = set.New(config.LocalCIDRs...).UnsortedList()
    76	
    77	        if gatewayMonitor.LeaseDuration == 0 {
    78	                gatewayMonitor.LeaseDuration = 20 * time.Second
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        if gatewayMonitor.RenewDeadline == 0 {
    82	                gatewayMonitor.RenewDeadline = 15 * time.Second
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        if gatewayMonitor.RetryPeriod == 0 {
    86	                gatewayMonitor.RetryPeriod = 2 * time.Second
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        gatewayMonitor.leaderElectionInfo.Store(&LeaderElectionInfo{})
    90	
    91	        var err error
    92	
    93	        gatewayMonitor.pFilter, err = packetfilter.New(k8snet.IPv4)
    94	        if err != nil {
    95	                return nil, errors.Wrap(err, "error creating packetfilter")
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        nodeName, ok := os.LookupEnv("NODE_NAME")
    99	        if !ok {
   100	                return nil, errors.New("error reading the NODE_NAME from the environment")
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        gatewayMonitor.nodeName = nodeName
   104	
   105	        cniIface, err := cni.Discover(gatewayMonitor.LocalClusterCIDRs, k8snet.IPv4)
   106	        if err == nil {
   107	                gatewayMonitor.cniIP = cniIface.IPAddress
   108	
   109	                logger.Infof("Discovered CNI interface IP %q", gatewayMonitor.cniIP)
   110	        } else {
   111	                logger.Errorf(err, "Error obtaining CNI IP address - health check functionality will not work")
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        gatewayMonitor.syncerConfig = &syncer.ResourceSyncerConfig{
   115	                SourceClient:    config.Client,
   116	                SourceNamespace: corev1.NamespaceAll,
   117	                Direction:       syncer.RemoteToLocal,
   118	                RestMapper:      config.RestMapper,
   119	                Federator: federate.NewCreateOrUpdateFederator(federate.CreateOrUpdateOptions{
   120	                        Client:          config.Client,
   121	                        RestMapper:      config.RestMapper,
   122	                        TargetNamespace: corev1.NamespaceAll,
   123	                }),
   124	                Scheme: config.Scheme,
   125	        }
   126	
   127	        gatewayMonitor.gatewaySharedInformer, err = syncer.NewSharedInformer(
   128	                NewGatewayResourceSyncerConfig(gatewayMonitor.syncerConfig, config.Spec.Namespace))
   129	        if err != nil {
   130	                return nil, errors.Wrap(err, "error creating shared informer")
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        gatewayMonitor.gatewaySharedInformerStopCh = make(chan struct{})
   134	
   135	        registry, err := event.NewRegistry(ctx, "globalnet-registry", event.AnyNetworkPlugin, gatewayMonitor)
   136	        if err != nil {
   137	                return nil, errors.Wrap(err, "error creating event registry")
   138	        }
   139	
   140	        return &gatewayMonitorInterface{monitor: gatewayMonitor, registry: registry}, nil
   141	}
   142	
   143	func (g *gatewayMonitorInterface) Start() error {
   144	        logger.Info("Starting GatewayMonitor to monitor the active Gateway node in the cluster.")
   145	
   146	        err := g.monitor.startLocalGatewayCleanupController()
   147	        if err != nil {
   148	                return err
   149	        }
   150	
   151	        go func() {
   152	                g.monitor.gatewaySharedInformer.Run(g.monitor.gatewaySharedInformerStopCh)
   153	        }()
   154	
   155	        eventController, err := controller.New(&controller.Config{
   156	                Registry:   g.registry,
   157	                RestMapper: g.monitor.RestMapper,
   158	                Client:     g.monitor.Client,
   159	                Scheme:     g.monitor.Scheme,
   160	        })
   161	        if err != nil {
   162	                return errors.Wrap(err, "error starting the event controller")
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        return eventController.Start(g.monitor.stopCh) //nolint // No need to wrap
   166	}
   167	
   168	func (g *gatewayMonitorInterface) Stop() {
   169	        _ = g.monitor.Stop()
   170	}
   171	
   172	func (g *gatewayMonitor) GetName() string {
   173	        return "GatewayMonitor"
   174	}
   175	
   176	func (g *gatewayMonitor) GetNetworkPlugins() []string {
   177	        return []string{event.AnyNetworkPlugin}
   178	}
   179	
   180	func (g *gatewayMonitor) Init(_ context.Context) error {
   181	        return g.createNATChain(chains.SmGlobalnetMark)
   182	}
   183	
   184	func (g *gatewayMonitor) Stop() error {
   185	        logger.Info("GatewayMonitor stopping")
   186	
   187	        g.shuttingDown.Store(true)
   188	
   189	        g.baseController.Stop()
   190	
   191	        // stopControllers should be pretty quick but put a deadline on it, so we don't block shutdown for a long time.
   192	
   193	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 10*time.Second)
   194	        defer cancel()
   195	
   196	        g.stopControllers(ctx, true)
   197	
   198	        close(g.gatewaySharedInformerStopCh)
   199	
   200	        return nil
   201	}
   202	
   203	func (g *gatewayMonitor) TransitionToGateway() error {
   204	        remoteEndpoints := g.State().GetRemoteEndpoints()
   205	        for i := range remoteEndpoints {
   206	                g.markRemoteClusterTraffic(AddRules, remoteEndpoints[i].Spec.Subnets...)
   207	        }
   208	
   209	        configureTCPMTUProbe()
   210

   211	
   212	        stopCh := ctx.Done()
   213	
   214	        err = ctl.Start(stopCh)
   215	        logger.FatalOnError(err, "Error starting controller")
   216	
   217	        cleanupLegacyIptables(env.ClusterCidr)
   218	
   219	        <-stopCh
   220	        ctl.Stop()
   221	
   222	        logger.Info("All controllers stopped or exited. Stopping submariner-route-agent")
   223	}

   212

   216	func (g *gatewayMonitor) TransitionToNonGateway() error {
   217	        g.stopControllers(context.Background(), true)
   218	        return nil
   219	}
   220	
   221	func (g *gatewayMonitor) RemoteEndpointCreated(endpoint *v1.Endpoint) error {
   222	        logger.V(log.DEBUG).Infof("Endpoint %q, host: %q belongs to a remote cluster",
   223	                endpoint.Spec.ClusterID, endpoint.Spec.Hostname)
   224	
   225	        globalCIDR := g.GatewayMonitorConfig.Spec.GlobalCIDR[0]
   226	
   227	        overlap, err := cidr.IsOverlapping(endpoint.Spec.Subnets, globalCIDR)
   228	        if err != nil {
   229	                // Ideally this case will never hit, as the subnets are valid CIDRs
   230	                logger.Warningf("unable to validate overlapping Service CIDR: %s", err)
   231	        }
   232	
   233	        if overlap {
   234	                // When GlobalNet is used, globalCIDRs allocated to the clusters should not overlap.
   235	                // If they overlap, skip the endpoint as its an invalid configuration which is not supported.
   236	                logger.Errorf(nil, "GlobalCIDR %q of local cluster %q overlaps with remote cluster %s",
   237	                        globalCIDR, g.GatewayMonitorConfig.Spec.ClusterID, endpoint.Spec.ClusterID)
   238	
   239	                return nil
   240	        }
   241	
   242	        g.markRemoteClusterTraffic(AddRules, endpoint.Spec.Subnets...)
   243	
   244	        return nil
   245	}
   246	
   247	func (g *gatewayMonitor) RemoteEndpointUpdated(endpoint *v1.Endpoint) error {
   248	        return g.RemoteEndpointCreated(endpoint)
   249	}
   250	
   251	func (g *gatewayMonitor) RemoteEndpointRemoved(endpoint *v1.Endpoint) error {
   252	        logger.V(log.DEBUG).Infof("Gateway monitor informed of removed endpoint: %v", endpoint)
   253	
   254	        // Endpoint associated with remote cluster is removed, delete the associated flows.
   255	        g.markRemoteClusterTraffic(DeleteRules, endpoint.Spec.Subnets...)
   256	
   257	        return nil
   258	}
   259	
   260	func (g *gatewayMonitor) startLeaderElection() {
   261	        if g.shuttingDown.Load() {
   262	                return
   263	        }
   264	
   265	        g.controllersMutex.Lock()
   266	        defer g.controllersMutex.Unlock()
   267	
   268	        // Usually when leadership is lost it's due to transition to a non-gateway however if it's due to renewal failure then we try to regain
   269	        // leadership in which case we'll still be on the gateway. Hence the isGatewayNode check here.
   270	        if !g.State().IsOnGateway() {
   271	                return
   272	        }
   273	
   274	        ctx, stop := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
   275	
   276	        leaderElectionInfo := &LeaderElectionInfo{
   277	                stopFunc: stop,
   278	                stopped:  make(chan struct{}),
   279	        }
   280	
   281	        g.leaderElectionInfo.Store(leaderElectionInfo)
   282	
   283	        logger.Info("On Gateway node - starting leader election")
   284	
   285	        lock, err := resourcelock.New(resourcelock.LeasesResourceLock, g.GatewayMonitorConfig.Spec.Namespace, LeaderElectionLockName,
   286	                g.KubeClient.CoreV1(), g.KubeClient.CoordinationV1(), resourcelock.ResourceLockConfig{
   287	                        Identity: g.nodeName + "-submariner-gateway",
   288	                })
   289	        utilruntime.Must(err)
   290	
   291	        go leaderelection.RunOrDie(ctx, leaderelection.LeaderElectionConfig{
   292	                Lock:            lock,
   293	                LeaseDuration:   g.LeaseDuration,
   294	                RenewDeadline:   g.RenewDeadline,
   295	                RetryPeriod:     g.RetryPeriod,
   296	                ReleaseOnCancel: true,
   297	                Callbacks: leaderelection.LeaderCallbacks{
   298	                        OnStartedLeading: func(_ context.Context) {
   299	                                err := g.startControllers() //nolint:contextcheck // Intentional to not pass context
   300	                                if err != nil {
   301	                                        logger.Error(err, "Error starting the controllers - stopping leader election")
   302	                                        leaderElectionInfo.stop()
   303	                                }
   304	                        },
   305	                        OnStoppedLeading: func() {
   306	                                logger.Info("Leader election stopped")
   307	
   308	                                close(leaderElectionInfo.stopped)
   309	
   310	                                // We may have lost leadership due to failed renewal and not gateway node transition or shutdown, in which case we want to
   311	                                // try to regain leadership. We also stop the controllers in case there's a gateway transition during the time that
   312	                                // leadership is lost and a new instance is able to contact the API server to acquire the lock. This avoids a potential
   313	                                // window where both instances are running should this instance finally observe the gateway transition. Note that we don't
   314	                                // clear the globalnet chains to avoid datapath disruption should leadership be regained.
   315	                                if !g.shuttingDown.Load() && g.State().IsOnGateway() {
   316	                                        g.stopControllers(context.Background(), false)
   317	                                        g.startLeaderElection()
   318	                                }
   319	                        },
   320	                },
   321	        })
   322	}
   323	
   324	//nolint:gocyclo // Ignore cyclomatic complexity here
   325	func (g *gatewayMonitor) startControllers() error {
   326	        g.controllersMutex.Lock()
   327	        defer g.controllersMutex.Unlock()
   328	
   329	        // Since this is called asynchronously when leadership is gained, check that we're still on the gateway node and that we're
   330	        // not shutting down. Also, we may have regained leadership so ensure the controllers weren't already started.
   331	        if g.shuttingDown.Load() || !g.State().IsOnGateway() || len(g.controllers) > 0 {
   332	                return nil
   333	        }
   334	
   335	        logger.Info("Starting controllers")

    46	        logger.Info("Transitioned to non-Gateway, cleaning up the IPsec xfrm rules")
    47	
    48	        errv6 := netlink.DeleteXfrmRules(k8snet.IPv6)
    49	        errv4 := netlink.DeleteXfrmRules(k8snet.IPv4)

    34	}
    35	
    36	var logger = log.Logger{Logger: logf.Log.WithName("CableDriver")}
    37	
    38	func NewVXLANCleanup() event.Handler {
    39	        return &vxlanCleanup{}
    40	}
    41	
    42	func (h *vxlanCleanup) GetNetworkPlugins() []string {
    43	        return []string{event.AnyNetworkPlugin}
    44	}

    46	func (h *vxlanCleanup) GetName() string {
    47	        return "VXLAN cleanup handler"
    48	}
    49	
    50	func (h *vxlanCleanup) TransitionToNonGateway() error {
    51	        logger.Infof("Cleaning up the routes")
    52	
    53	        errv6 := netlink.DeleteIfaceAndAssociatedRoutes(vxlan.GetVxlanInterfaceName(k8snet.IPv6), vxlan.TableID, k8snet.IPv6)
    54	        errv4 := netlink.DeleteIfaceAndAssociatedRoutes(vxlan.GetVxlanInterfaceName(k8snet.IPv4), vxlan.TableID, k8snet.IPv4)
    55	
    56	        return errors.Join(errv6, errv4)
    57	}
